Anima Thief

Active Return to Cheong-woon
Master Level 1
Description Return to Cheong-woon Valley.
Level 1 Returns you to Cheong-woon Valley.
Cooldown: 600 sec


Active Shapeshift
Master Level 1
Description Hides your Anima ears, tail, and stripes to conceal where you're from.
Use the skill again to restore these features.
Not shown by default in some UI.
Level 1 Hides your ears, tail, and face stripes.
Cooldown: 10 sec


Active Exclusive Spell
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby characters.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: +4%, Duration: 40 min


Passive Spirit Affinity
Master Level 1
Description Harness your natural affinity as an Anima to increase the duration of your summons.
Level 1 Minion Duration +10%


Passive Fiend Seal
Master Level 10
Description As Taotie devours more spirits, his power grows... and so does yours.
Level 1 Attack Power: +1%, Final Damage: +1%
10 Attack Power: +10%, Final Damage: +10%


Passive Bravado
Master Level 2
Description You're confident even in the face of the strongest enemy. Ignore a portion of your enemy's Defense and inflict more damage against enemies that have full HP.
Level 1 Enemy DEF Ignored: +5%, Damage +9% against enemies with 100% HP
2 Enemy DEF Ignored: +10%, Damage +14% against enemies with 100% HP

Hoyoung (I)

Passive Talisman Energy
Master Level 1
Description Successful hits with your Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills charge your Talisman Energy, up to a maximum of 100. You can use Talisman Energy to use Talisman skills.
Right-click to toggle the visual effect for Talisman Energy's full charge.
Level 1


Active Humanity: As-You-Will Fan
Master Level 20
Description [Humanity Skill] Swings a massive fan. Enemies hit directly by the fan take greater damage.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 52%, Number of Attacks: 5 times, Against Enemies Struck by Fan: Final Damage +5%
20 MP Cost: 16, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 90%, Number of Attacks: 5 times, Against Enemies Struck by Fan: Final Damage +5%


Active Talisman: Evil-Sealing Gourd
Master Level 20
Description [Talisman Skill] Summons a gourd that sucks up enemies. Press the skill key a second time to launch any enemies captured by the gourd.
Cannot swallow boss monsters, stationary monsters, or enemies 11+ levels higher than you. If you wait too long after sucking up enemies, you will be unable to launch them from the gourd.
Level 1 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, Max Enemies Swallowed: 4. Launch swallowed enemies by pressing the skill key again.
Attacks up to 6 enemies that are absorbed or within range of the launch attack for 155% damage 6 times.
Boss Damage: +20%.
20 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, Max Enemies Swallowed: 4. Launch swallowed enemies by pressing the skill key again.
Attacks up to 6 enemies that are absorbed or within range of the launch attack for 250% damage 6 times.
Boss Damage: +20%.


Active Graceful Flight
Master Level 5
Description Leap with such grace that you could balance on a single blade of grass. Use while midair to jump. Can be used twice before touching the ground again.
When Graceful Flight is used to jump up, Nimbus Cloud's flight time is limited.
If the Nimbus Cloud lock command feature is active, it can be used with the up arrow key to move up.
The jump distance and height increase with the skill level.
Level 1 MP Cost: 13, allows you to jump a greater distance
5 MP Cost: 5, allows you to jump a greater distance


Active Nimbus Cloud
Master Level 1
Description You faced a great trial and gained the power to summon the Nimbus Cloud.
Hold down the skill key while airborne or hold down the up arrow and jump keys together to mount the Nimbus Cloud. While on the Nimbus Cloud, use the arrow keys to fly.
Flight time decreases when used after Graceful Flight up is used.
Right-click to lock command.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10, Temporarily gain the power to fly
Can't use upward Graceful Flight after using Nimbus Cloud.


Passive Light Steps
Master Level 10
Description Harnesses mind-over-matter to make your body light and swift.
Level 1 Speed:+4, Max Speed: +2
10 Speed:+22, Max Speed: +20


Passive Shrouding Mist
Master Level 9
Description Protects you from enemy attacks as though you were enshrouded in mist.
Level 1 Avoidability +7%
9 Avoidability +15%


Hoyoung (II)

Active Earth: Ground-Shattering Wave
Master Level 20
Description [Earth Skill] Kicks the ground to unleash a shockwave along the surface. Can only be used while on the ground.

After casting, press the forward arrow key and the skill key again to link into Ground-Shattering Wave (True), charging forward. If you do not do this, it will link into Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone) instead.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Damage: 62%, Number of Attacks: 4, Max Enemies Hit: 6
20 MP Cost: 40, Damage: 100%, Number of Attacks: 4, Max Enemies Hit: 6


Active Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone/True)
Master Level 20
Description This skill shares its skill level with Earth: Ground-Shattering Wave.. Ride a shockwave to charge forward.

Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 After using Earth: Ground-Shattering Wave, you can link into Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone) or Ground-Shattering Wave (True), Attacks up to 6 enemies with 62% damage 4 times.
20 After using Earth: Ground-Shattering Wave, you can link into Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone) or Ground-Shattering Wave (True), Attacks up to 6 enemies with 100% damage 4 times.


Active Talisman: Clone
Master Level 20
Description [Talisman Skill] Conjures a clone to trick enemies with sly attacks. For the duration of this skill, when you attack enemies, a clone will appear and attack nearby enemies.
Attacks from installation skills or summoned minions will not create a clone.

Talisman: Clone is unaffected by attack reflection, and targets the boss with the highest HP first.
Level 1 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, For 162 sec, create 3 clone(s) when attacking, Each clone attacks for 50% damage 4 times, Damage against Normal Monsters: +20%
Clone creation has a 1.5 sec cooldown
20 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, For 200 sec, create 3 clone(s) when attacking, Each clone attacks for 60% damage 4 times, Damage against Normal Monsters: +20%
Clone creation has a 1.5 sec cooldown


Active Ritual Fan Acceleration
Master Level 10
Description Uses MP to increase the attack speed of your Ritual Fan for a short time.
Required Skill: Ritual Fan Mastery Lv. 5
Level 1 MP Cost: 28, Duration: 164 sec, Ritual Fan Attack Speed: +2
10 MP Cost: 10, Duration: 200 sec, Ritual Fan Attack Speed: +2


Passive Ritual Fan Mastery
Master Level 10
Description Increases Ritual Fan Mastery and Attack Power.
Level 10 required to learn Advanced Ritual Fan Mastery.
Level 1 Ritual Fan Mastery: +14%, Attack Power: +7
10 Ritual Fan Mastery: +50%, Attack Power: +25


Passive Out of Sight
Master Level 10
Description After a clone attack, hide yourself in darkness. While hidden, you cannot be hit by enemies. Using an attack skill will reveal you. Using attack skills will not reveal you (excludes class-wide skills).
Level 1 Using Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone), Stone Tremor (Clone), Iron Fan Gale (Clone), or Consuming Flames (Clone) will hide you for 2 sec. Using an attack skill while hidden will reveal you.
If you dodge an attack that deals damage proportional to Max HP, your remaining time to hide will be reduced by 20% of the maximum.
[Passive Effects: Avoidability +2%]
10 Using Ground-Shattering Wave (Clone), Stone Tremor (Clone), Iron Fan Gale (Clone), or Consuming Flames (Clone) will hide you for 2 sec. Using an attack skill while hidden will reveal you.
If you dodge an attack that deals damage proportional to Max HP, your remaining time to hide will be reduced by 20% of the maximum.
[Passive Effects: Avoidability +20%]


Passive Third Eye
Master Level 10
Description Opens your mind's eye, allowing you to see through the enemies' weaknesses.
Level 1 Critical Rate: +3%, Critical Damage: +1%
10 Critical Rate: +30%, Critical Damage: +10%


Passive Heavenly Body
Master Level 9
Description Attunes your bodies to the heavens, granting greater control over Nimbus Cloud.
Level 1 Jump: +4
Increases the duration and flight speed for the Nimbus Cloud skill
9 Jump: +20
Increases the duration and flight speed for the Nimbus Cloud skill


Passive Fortune Fitness
Master Level 5
Description Your fitness increases Luck and Final Damage.
Level 1 Luck: +12, Final Damage: +1%
5 Luck: +60, Final Damage: +5%

Hoyoung (III)

Passive Scroll Energy
Master Level 1
Description Your master's spell book has taught you to use Scroll Skills.
Successful hits with your Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, or use of Talisman Skills, will earn you Scroll Energy, which powers your Scroll Skills.

You can hold a maximum of 900 Scroll Energy.
Level 1


Active Heaven: Iron Fan Gale
Master Level 20
Description [Heaven Skill] Summons a giant fan to blow a gale downward.
Press the forward key and the skill key again to use Iron Fan Gale (True), leaping forward. Otherwise, this skill will link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone), sending a clone to attack. This skill's attack speed cannot be increased beyond a set value.
Level 1 MP Cost: 35, Damage: 131%, Number of Attacks: 5, Max Enemies Hit: 6
20 MP Cost: 45, Damage: 150%, Number of Attacks: 5, Max Enemies Hit: 6


Active Iron Fan Gale (Clone/True)
Master Level 20
Description This skill shares its skill level with Heaven: Iron Fan Gale.. After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, leaps forward to stomp on enemies.
A successful Iron Fan Gale (True) attack will cause you to rebound off the enemy back into the air.

Iron Fan Gale (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, you can link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone) or Iron Fan Gale (True), After touching an enemy, attacks up to 6 enemies with 131% damage 5 times
20 After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, you can link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone) or Iron Fan Gale (True), After touching an enemy, attacks up to 6 enemies with 150% damage 5 times


Active Earth: Stone Tremor
Master Level 20
Description [Earth Skill] Slams the ground hard, causing massive stones to jut out from the earth. Can only be used while on ground.

Press the left or right arrow key along with the skill key again to link into Stone Tremor (True), teleporting in that direction. If you do not link into Stone Tremor (True), it will link into Stone Tremor (Clone) and send a clone to attack, instead.
Level 1 MP Cost: 51, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 142%, Number of Attacks: 6, Stun Duration for Normal Monsters: 5 sec
Cooldown: 6 sec
20 MP Cost: 70, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 180%, Number of Attacks: 6, Stun Duration for Normal Monsters: 5 sec
Cooldown: 6 sec


Active Stone Tremor (Clone/True)
Master Level 20
Description This skill shares its skill level with Earth: Stone Tremor. After using Earth: Stone Tremor, teleports to one end of the rock outcropping and shatters it.
When using Stone Tremor (True), you can use the arrow keys to select whether you move left or right. When using Stone Tremor (Clone), you will only move forward.
Stone Tremor (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 After using Earth: Stone Tremor, you can link into Stone Tremor (Clone) or Stone Tremor (True), Teleports to the edge of the rock outcropping and attacks up to 10 enemies for 142% damage 6 times.
20 After using Earth: Stone Tremor, you can link into Stone Tremor (Clone) or Stone Tremor (True), Teleports to the edge of the rock outcropping and attacks up to 10 enemies for 180% damage 6 times.


Active Talisman: Seeking Ghost Flame
Master Level 20
Description [Talisman Skill] Conjures a living flame to chase and attack enemies. The flame attacks a target, pauses in place, and then finds a new target to attack.

Seeking Ghost Flame is unaffected by attack reflection, and targets the boss with the highest HP first.
Level 1 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, Flame Summon Duration: 90 sec, Enemy Targeting Interval: 1.8 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 172%, Number of Attacks: 5
20 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, Flame Summon Duration: 90 sec, Enemy Targeting Interval: 1.8 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 210%, Number of Attacks: 5
Show/hide all levels
Active Scroll: Degeneration
Master Level 20
Description [Scroll Skill] A mysterious light shines from your scroll, transforming enemies into frogs, bugs, and other vermin. When the light touches an enemy, it is reflected onto other nearby enemies, transforming a multitude of enemies. Boss monsters cannot be transformed.
Level 1 Scroll Energy Cost: 900, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 336%, Number of Attacks: 8, Boss Damage: +20%
Transformation Duration (Normal Enemies Only): 60 sec, Enemy DEF: -20%.
20 Scroll Energy Cost: 900, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 450%, Number of Attacks: 8, Boss Damage: +20%
Transformation Duration (Normal Enemies Only): 60 sec, Enemy DEF: -20%.

Hoyoung (IV)

Show/hide all levels
Active Heaven: Consuming Flames
Master Level 30
Description [Heaven Skill] Fans the flames of destruction. Can only be used while airborne.
Press the up arrow key and skill key again to link into Consuming Flames (True), launching yourself further into the air. If you do not link into Consuming Flames (True), it will link into Consuming Flames (Clone), sending a clone instead.
Not affected by cooldown reset. This skill's attack speed cannot be increased beyond a set value.
Level 1 MP Cost: 61, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 312%, Number of Attacks: 6, Usage of Graceful Flight and Nimbus Cloud is reset after using this skill
Cooldown: 8 sec
30 MP Cost: 90, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 370%, Number of Attacks: 6, Usage of Graceful Flight and Nimbus Cloud is reset after using this skill
Cooldown: 8 sec
31 MP Cost: 91, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 372%, Number of Attacks: 6, Usage of Graceful Flight and Nimbus Cloud is reset after using this skill
Cooldown: 8 sec
32 MP Cost: 92, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 374%, Number of Attacks: 6, Usage of Graceful Flight and Nimbus Cloud is reset after using this skill
Cooldown: 8 sec
Active Heaven: Consuming Flames
Master Level 30
Description [Heaven Skill] Fans the flames of destruction. Can only be used while airborne.
Press the up arrow key and skill key again to link into Consuming Flames (True), launching yourself further into the air. If you do not link into Consuming Flames (True), it will link into Consuming Flames (Clone), sending a clone instead.
Not affected by cooldown reset. This skill's attack speed cannot be increased beyond a set value.

Active Talisman: Warp Gate
Master Level 20
Description [Talisman Skill] Summons a warp gate. Press the skill key again while the gate is active to mark your location and teleport to the gate.
Use the skill again while near the gate to teleport back to your marked location.
Pressing up and the skill key while the gate is open consumes Talisman Energy, opening a new gate while the existing warp gate and marked location vanish.
Level 1 Talisman Energy Cost: 100, Warp Gate Duration: 62 sec
Using the skill again teleports you to the gate, Using the skill near the gate teleports you to your previous location. Teleport and Opening a New Gate Cooldown: 5 sec
[Passive Effect: Avoidability Chance: +1%]

[Passive Effect: Avoidability Chance: +20%]

Active Scroll: Star Vortex
Master Level 30
Description [Scroll Skill] Summons a powerful vortex that absorbs the enemies' energy. Use the skill again to make the vortex disappear. Restores HP and MP to party members based on how many enemies are hit.

Scroll: Star Vortex is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 Scroll Energy Cost: 900, Creates a vortex that deals 140% damage 6 times for 40 sec
You can absorb 1 energy for every 4 successful hits up to 9, Attacking boss monsters absorbs 3 times the energy
Using the skill again will make the vortex disappear and restore 5% of the Max HP and Max MP of party member for each energy absorbed.

Active Sage: Dream of Shangri-La
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description Transports you into a scroll featuring a beautiful vista, giving you a moment of respite in battle.
If you don't use the full skill duration, then this skill's cooldown will be reduced. Not affected by effects which which reset or reduce cooldown.
Can be used while airborne or while using 1st to 4th job skills, but can only be activated during the finishing hit of Humanity: Gold-Banded Cudgel.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10% of Max MP, Invincible while casting and while holding down the key, Max Skill Duration: 20 sec
When the skill effects end, cooldown is reduced by 9.3 sec for each second of remaining duration.
Cooldown: 200 sec


Active Sage: Tai Yu Clone
Level Requirement 190
Master Level 1
Description Transforms one of your clones into a clone of your master, who then proceeds to nag your enemies' ears off. Stuns targets.

Targets cannot be stunned by Sage: Tai Yu Clone or other skills again for 90 sec.
Level 1 MP Cost: 200, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 800%, Number of Attacks: 8
Stun Duration: 11 sec
Stun duration can increase up to 100% based on the damage inflicted with the attack.
Cooldown: 180 sec


Active Sage: Tai Yu's Miracle Tonic
Level Requirement 140
Master Level 1
Description Takes a sip of medicine stolen from your master's stash. Talisman Energy and Scroll Energy are completely restored after taking the medicine and aren't consumed for a period of time.
Restores Talisman Energy and Scroll Energy over time.
Not affected by cooldown reset.
Level 1 MP Cost: 800. Completely restores Talisman and Scroll Energy as soon as it's used. For 3 sec, Talisman and Scroll Energy aren't used.
For 9 sec, periodically restores Talisman Energy by 35 and Scroll Energy by 350.
Cooldown: 90 sec

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.
25 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 300%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 120 sec.
30 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 330%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 100 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Master Level 25

Active Lotus Flower
Master Level 25
Description Summon a lotus flower with an auspicious power. When you are hit by a fatal attack within a certain range around the lotus, the blessing of the lotus allows you to be revived inside the lotus instead of dying. Cannot be used while the Heaven's Door buff is active. If you receive a Heaven's Door buff while the lotus is summoned, the lotus will disappear.
Level 1 MP Cost: 15% of Max MP, Lotus Summon Duration: 1655 sec.
Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.
Cooldown: 400 sec. Skill Cooldown upon successful revival: +1545 sec.

Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.
Cooldown: 400 sec. Skill Cooldown upon successful revival: +1425 sec.

Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.

Active Grandis Goddess's Blessing
Master Level 25
Description The goddess of Grandis has a different appearance for each of her child races, and she grants a different blessing to each race. Affected by effects which reduce cooldown.
Level 1 HP Cost: 800, Duration: 40 sec.
Nova: Skills have a 40% chance to bypass cooldown as many as 3 time(s).
Damage: +6%
Kaiser receives an additional 5% Damage increase for each Morph Gauge stage.
Flora: Excluding your weapon, 42% of your equipment's Attack Power & Magic ATT, whichever you do not use, is converted to the one you do use. Any set effects do not apply. The converted bonus cannot exceed 150% of the weapon's base Attack Power or Magic ATT, whichever one you use.
Attack Power and Magic ATT: +13
Anima: Damage: +11%
Hoyoung: Talisman and Scroll Energy Charge: + 46%, Lara: Increases Final Damage Increase to 6% upon activating Dragon Vein Echo.

Active Venom Burst
Master Level 25
Description Causes the poison inflicting nearby enemies to burst and spread.
Level 1 MP Cost: 300. Consumes all active Damage-Over-Time stacks on up to 12 poisoned enemies in range, and instantly inflicts 100% of their remaining damage, plus an additional 520% damage 6 times.
Additional damage is +15% per remaining second of consumed DoT stacks, up to 5
Afterwards, spreads the original DoT damage across up to 10 nearby enemies
Cooldown: 8 sec.

Active Last Resort
Master Level 25
Description You vow to destroy your enemies at any cost. You can renew your vow to empower its effects by using the skill again while it's active. Using the skill with the down arrow key will immediately renew your vow. With Action Customization enabled, you can renew your vow by pressing its key again, without use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, reduces Avoidability (including Bonus Evasion) and increases Final Damage for 30 sec, Hit Damage increased if attacked within a certain percentage of your max HP.
Enters 2nd Stage with remaining duration being reduced to 50% when skill is used again during 1st Stage, skill ends when used again during 2nd Stage.
1st Stage - Avoidability: -20%, Hit Damage: +10%, Final Damage: +10%
2nd Stage - Avoidability: -90%, Hit Damage: +30%, Final Damage: +24%
Cooldown: 90 sec

Class-Specific Skills

Show/hide all levels
Active Sage: Clone Rampage
Master Level 25
Description Draws out the full power of Talisman: Clone, raining a barrage of clones on enemies. Greatly increases the Attack Power and number of clones created with Talisman: Clone. While Sage: Clone Rampage is active, the clones target the boss with the highest HP first.
Can only be used while Talisman: Clone is active. While this skill is active, Talisman: Clone's duration will not decrease.
Required Skill: Talisman: Clone Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, For 30 sec, create 10 clone(s) when attacking, Each clone attacks for 208%p more damage than Talisman: Clone 4 times
Clone creation has a 1.5 sec cooldown
Cooldown: 180 sec
25 MP Cost: 1000, For 30 sec, create 10 clone(s) when attacking, Each clone attacks for 400%p more damage than Talisman: Clone 4 times
Clone creation has a 1.5 sec cooldown
Cooldown: 180 sec
30 MP Cost: 1000, For 30 sec, create 10 clone(s) when attacking, Each clone attacks for 440%p more damage than Talisman: Clone 4 times
Clone creation has a 1.5 sec cooldown
Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Scroll: Tiger of Songyu
Master Level 25
Description [Scroll Skill] Summons the guardian of Mt. Songyu, a giant tiger spirit. Whenever you achieve an attribute combo stage 3, the tiger gives out a mighty roar to shake heaven, earth, and your enemies.
Scroll: Tiger of Songyu is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 Scroll Energy Cost: 900, Duration: 45 sec., Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 936%, Number of Attacks: 8.
When you reach attribute combo stage 3, its next attack will replace the normal attack with a roar that periodically deals 364% damage 4 times.
Tiger's attacks have a cooldown of 3 sec.
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Active Sage: Wrath of Gods
Master Level 25
Description Call upon the gods of an unknown place and time. Temporarily increases your damage, with the gods joining in after every few attacks.
Use the skill a second time to summon the gods' full power in a massive attack.

Sage: Wrath of Gods is unaffected by attack reflection, and targets the boss with the highest HP first.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000. Duration: 30 sec. Damage: +22%
The gods strike once per 12 successful attacks, hitting up to 10 enemies for 884% damage 8 times. Cooldown: 1.5 sec.
Using the skill again will immediately end its effects and summon the gods again at once, creating 6 shockwave(s) and hitting up to 15 enemies for 1040% damage 15 times.
You are invincible while summoning the gods. This skill negates attack ignore and attack reflection effects.
Upon summoning the gods, damage for Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, as well as Clone/True skills, increases by 20% for 30 sec.
Cooldown: 180 sec.
25 MP Cost: 1000. Duration: 30 sec. Damage: +70%
The gods strike once per 12 successful attacks, hitting up to 10 enemies for 1700% damage 8 times. Cooldown: 1.5 sec.
Using the skill again will immediately end its effects and summon the gods again at once, creating 6 shockwave(s) and hitting up to 15 enemies for 2000% damage 15 times.
You are invincible while summoning the gods. This skill negates attack ignore and attack reflection effects.
Upon summoning the gods, damage for Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, as well as Clone/True skills, increases by 20% for 30 sec.
Cooldown: 180 sec.
30 MP Cost: 1000. Duration: 30 sec. Damage: +80%
The gods strike once per 12 successful attacks, hitting up to 10 enemies for 1870% damage 8 times. Cooldown: 1.5 sec.
Using the skill again will immediately end its effects and summon the gods again at once, creating 6 shockwave(s) and hitting up to 15 enemies for 2200% damage 15 times.
You are invincible while summoning the gods. This skill negates attack ignore and attack reflection effects.
Upon summoning the gods, damage for Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, as well as Clone/True skills, increases by 20% for 30 sec.
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.

Description [Heaven Skill] Fans the flames of destruction. Can only be used while airborne.
Press the up arrow key and skill key again to link into Consuming Flames (True), launching yourself further into the air. If you do not link into Consuming Flames (True), it will link into Consuming Flames (Clone), sending a clone instead.
A flame emblem is created upon use, and explodes on the spot after a set number of attacks land.
Not affected by cooldown reset. This skill's attack speed cannot be increased beyond a set value.
Required Skill: Heaven: Consuming Flames Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 607%, Number of Attacks: 6, Usage of Graceful Flight and Nimbus Cloud is reset after using this skill
Flame Emblem Duration: 15 sec, the flame explodes on the spot when 3 attacks from Hoyoung land, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 511%, Number of Attacks: 5
Cooldown: 8 sec

Passive HEXA Consuming Flames (Clone/True)
Master Level 30
Description This skill shares its skill level with Heaven: Consuming Flames. After using Heaven: Consuming Flames, soar into the air and create a burst of fire.
Consuming Flames (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Required Skill: Heaven: Consuming Flames Lv. 30
Level 1 After using Heaven: Consuming Flames, you can link into Consuming Flames (Clone) or Consuming Flames (True), Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 410%, Number of Attacks: 6
30 After using Heaven: Consuming Flames, you can link into Consuming Flames (Clone) or Consuming Flames (True), Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 555%, Number of Attacks: 6

Active HEXA Earth: Stone Tremor
Master Level 30
Description [Earth Skill] Slams the ground hard, causing massive stones to jut out from the earth. Can only be used while on ground.
Press the left or right arrow key along with the skill key again to link into Stone Tremor (True), teleporting in that direction. If you do not link into Stone Tremor (True), it will link into Stone Tremor (Clone) and send a clone to attack, instead.
Required Skill: Earth: Stone Tremor Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 90, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 476%, Number of Attacks: 6, Stun Duration for Normal Enemies: 5 sec
Cooldown: 6 sec
30 MP Cost: 105, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 650%, Number of Attacks: 6, Stun Duration for Normal Enemies: 5 sec
Cooldown: 6 sec

Active HEXA Earth: Stone Tremor (Enhanced)
Master Level 30
Description [Earth Skill] Slams the ground hard, causing massive stones to jut out from the earth. Can only be used while on ground.
Press the left or right arrow key along with the skill key again to link into Stone Tremor (True), teleporting in that direction. If you do not link into Stone Tremor (True), it will link into Stone Tremor (Clone) and send a clone to attack, instead.
Required Skill: Earth: Stone Tremor Lv. 20

Passive HEXA Stone Tremor (Clone/True)
Master Level 30
Description This skill shares its skill level with Earth: Stone Tremor. After using Earth: Stone Tremor, teleports to one end of the rock outcropping and shatters it.
When using Stone Tremor (True), you can use the arrow keys to select whether you move left or right. When using Stone Tremor (Clone), you will only move forward.
Stone Tremor (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Required Skill: Earth: Stone Tremor Lv. 20
Level 1 After using Earth: Stone Tremor, you can link into Stone Tremor (Clone) or Stone Tremor (True), Teleports to the edge of the rock outcropping and attacks up to 10 enemies for 476% damage 6 times.
30 After using Earth: Stone Tremor, you can link into Stone Tremor (Clone) or Stone Tremor (True), Teleports to the edge of the rock outcropping and attacks up to 10 enemies for 650% damage 6 times.

Active Universal Harmony
Master Level 30
Description Enlightened by the harmony of all creation, uses enhanced Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills.
When you combo a certain number of Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, enhance the next Heaven: Consuming Flames, Earth: Stone Tremor, or Humanity: Gold-Banded Cudgel and temporarily increase their Final Damage.
Level 1 Upon reaching a stage 3 combo for Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills 3 times, enhances the next Heaven: HEXA Consuming Flames, HEXA Earth: Stone Tremor, or Humanity: Gold-Banded Cudgel
After using enhanced Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, Final Damage: +5% for 40 sec
Cooldown: 30 sec
30 Upon reaching a stage 3 combo for Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills 3 times, enhances the next Heaven: HEXA Consuming Flames, HEXA Earth: Stone Tremor, or Humanity: Gold-Banded Cudgel
After using enhanced Heaven, Earth, and Humanity skills, Final Damage: +10% for 40 sec
Cooldown: 30 sec

Active HEXA Heaven: Iron Fan Gale
Master Level 30
Description [Heaven Skill] Summon a giant fan to blow a gale downward.
Press the forward key and the skill key again to use
Iron Fan Gale (True), leaping forward. Otherwise, this skill
will link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone), sending a clone
to attack. This skill's attack speed cannot be increased
beyond a set value.
Required Skill: Heaven: Iron Fan Gale Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 50, Damage: 304%, Number of Attacks: 5, Max Enemies Hit: 6

Active HEXA Heaven: Iron Fan Gale (Clone/True)
Master Level 30
Description This skill shares its skill level with Heaven: Iron Fan Gale. After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, leap forward to stomp on enemies.
A successful Iron Fan Gale (True) attack will cause you to rebound off the enemy back into the air.

Iron Fan Gale (Clone) is unaffected by attack reflection.
Required Skill: Heaven: Iron Fan Gale Lv. 20
Level 1 After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, you can link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone) or Iron Fan Gale (True), After touching an enemy, attacks up to 6 enemies with 304% damage 5 times
30 After using Heaven: Iron Fan Gale, you can link into Iron Fan Gale (Clone) or Iron Fan Gale (True), After touching an enemy, attacks up to 6 enemies with 420% damage 5 times

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
